/get_cl23/cl_name get pt qry -> select  title as cl_title, id as id_cl from cl_23.anag_cl  where name ilike 'cl_fanghi'
{FANGHI DI DEPURAZIONE IN AGRICOLTURA 7}
get cl qry -> SELECT id, 7 as id_cl , prog, trim(sez) as sez, domanda, si_punti * peso as punti_si, no_punti * peso as punti_no, grp, comm, blocker, grp_block, risposta_block FROM cl_23.cl_fanghi order by prog

[INFO] 2024/06/21 10:37  Macros of N_id: %
get Mac qry -> select distinct 123 as m_id, desc_macroarea as m_desc, cod_macroarea m_code, 'codice_univoco' as m_cod_univ from cl_23.a_tipol_ml where codice_univoco is not null order by 2
[INFO] 2024/06/21 10:37  Aggrs of M_id: AUA
get Agg qry -> select distinct '-1' a_id, desc_aggregazione a_desc, cod_attivita a_code from cl_23.a_tipol_ml where cod_macroarea='AUA'
[INFO] 2024/06/21 10:37  Lda of A_id: ARIA
get LdA qry -> select codice_univoco l_id, desc_lda l_desc, cod_lda l_code from  cl_23.a_tipol_ml where cod_attivita = 'ARIA'

get_cls_pre executing -> select '-999' as l_id, allegati_categ  as c_name  from cl_23.a_tipol_ml where codice_univoco ilike '%AUA-ARIA-EMISSIONI%'
Cls: [{-999 cl_emissioni}][INFO] 2024/06/21 10:37  Cl of Lda_id: AUA-ARIA-EMISSIONI
/get_cls23/idlda() qry -> select ml.id::text as l_id, ml.codice_univoco as l_codice_univ, cl.name as c_name, cl.title as c_title from cl_23.a_tipol_ml ml left join cl_23.anag_cl cl on upper(trim(ml.allegati_categ))=upper(trim(cl.name)) where codice_univoco ilike '%AUA-ARIA-EMISSIONI%'

{EMISSIONI IN ATMOSFERA 3}
